Chapter 3001: Chapter 2999: Chatting About Three Bucks
“Perhaps, I understand why Daoist Priest Scarlet Heaven has insisted on cultivating a Heavenly Dao,” said the Great Northern Emperor, looking at Tyrannical Song, who was under the ‘Dao Rune’ at the time. He had suddenly resolved an inner perplexity.

After cultivating a ‘Heavenly Dao,’ in the Immortal Realm, one could be like the current Tyrannical Song!

In fact, not just Tyrannical Song, but also him, Daoist Priest Scarlet Heaven, Cheng Lin, Song Shuhang, master of the Buddha Temple, and the Eight-Armed Ancient Heavenly Demon—fellow friends who, if needed, could now contact Daozi and obtain a portion of the simplified ‘Sub-Immortal Information’ from him.

This is the benefit of having a Heavenly Dao as your backing.

At this moment, under the protection of the Heavenly Dao ‘Daozi,’ Tyrannical Song could behave as recklessly as he desired. The things he once did only cautiously, he could now do boldly and without worry!

“Agree, and then begin the one-on-one process,” the Great Northern Emperor said with a smile that seemed to melt icebergs.

The surrounding immortals nodded and selected the ‘agree’ option.

The entire ‘time-distorted secret realm’ quieted down.

The immortals and the Tyrannical Songs all closed their eyes without speaking a word.

If it were not for the intermittent puffing of white smoke over Song Shuhang’s head, this scene would appear as though time had stopped.

Pavilion Master Chu’s dumb hair was enveloped by white smoke, discontentedly shaking it off.

After a moment.

The bored Pavilion Master Chu used her dumb hair to encircle the white smoke, forming it into a smoke ball that she carefully stacked on top of the ‘Hamster Ball’ above Song Shuhang’s head, making it the upper half of a gourd.

“Perfect,” remarked Pavilion Master Chu’s dumb hair with satisfaction.

Just as she spoke, the Heavenly Dao protective runes above dispensed golden light, promptly cooling and reinforcing Tyrannical Song’s head.

The smoke ball that formed the upper half of the gourd also dispersed.

Pavilion Master Chu’s dumb hair: “!!!”

The smoke ball that I had so painstakingly formed, ah.

Pavilion Master Chu’s dumb hair lost its momentum and lazily lay on top of Song Shuhang’s head, motionless.

...

...

Elsewhere.

Evil Corpse Tyrannical Song arrived in the Sinful Black Lotus World, the iron fortress of Senior White Two.

“Senior White, has the egg of King Kun been born? My main body sent me here to borrow the egg of King Kun and see if I could extract some clues from it,” said the Evil Corpse with the same familiarity as visiting his own home, entering Senior White’s fortress.

“Still experimenting, wait on the side for a bit. Once I finish this experiment here, I’ll let you take the egg of King Kun away,” said one of Senior White Two’s research clones.

It’s unclear what contents Senior White Two’s clones are researching.

Could it be the ‘Egg of King Kun Cookbook’?

Unable to borrow the egg of King Kun for the time being, Evil Tyrant temporarily rested in the Sinful Black Lotus World.

As the experiment by Senior White Two took slightly longer... the idly bored Evil Tyrant began strolling around the vicinity of the Sinful Black Lotus World.

Walking around, he unconsciously left the Sinful Black Lotus World and went over to Dark Song’s place to visit the sealed fat ball leader.

At this time, Dark Song retained only a thread of Tyrannical Song’s consciousness, maintaining basic operations while stationed in the Demon Sea World.

The fat ball leader was pressed near the Demon Sea World by the Heavenly Dao Seal, guarded by Dark Song.

When Evil Tyrant arrived, he discovered that fat ball leader was in the middle of covertly analyzing the seal of Daozi.

The sealing technique of Daozi wasn’t too clever; it was a seal that purely overpowered finesse with force... suppressing directly with Heavenly Dao authority and rules.

“Long time no see, fat ball leader,” said Evil Tyrant as he sat down cross-legged near the seal.

The fat ball leader silently glanced at Song Shuhang’s Evil Corpse and chose not to speak.

Evil Tyrant didn’t mind.

After he had taken his seat, he spoke as if talking to himself, “Fat Ball, are you bored? Want to chat for five bucks?”

Fat Ball: “...”

Ba Er began talking on his own, “Before proving their Dao under the Will of the Heavens, the rulers of the Netherworld Realm were part of the Will of the Heavens itself, becoming masters of the Netherworld. So, that means the rulers of the Netherworld also possess a perfected path to immortality, right?”

Fat Ball: “...”

“So, what exactly is your path to immortality, Fat Ball?” Ba Er asked.

Fat Ball: “[Sneer] You think I’d tell you that?”

“Actually, whether you tell me or not doesn’t really matter. Once our preparations here are complete and my Dark Song merges with you, Fat Ball, I think I’ll eventually find out all these things,” Ba Er said cheerfully.

Being an Evil Corpse, and given that Tyrannical Song had so many heart-wrenching pendants nearby, Ba Er could learn quite a lot just by listening.

All Fat Ball wanted to do was swear inside, but because it had to remain civil, it couldn’t say those words out loud.

“By the way, Fat Ball... what’s your origin?” Ba Er asked again.

In the tale of grievances between the Sage of Confucianism and the eighth Heavenly Dao, whenever the origin of the Heavenly Dao liquefied metal ball is brought up, it’s described as ‘mysterious’.

No one knows the roots of the Heavenly Dao ball; it isn’t human, demon, monster, Buddha, or ghost...

And before its final battle with the Sage of Confucianism, no one knew its origin.

It seemed to have popped out of thin air.

Ba Er really wanted to try the “secret appraisal technique” on Fat Ball—now that the main body had reached the Immortal Realm, the cost of appraising a ruler of the Netherworld should be greatly reduced.

But considering that the main body was currently in a ‘multi-threaded simultaneous cultivation discussion’ state, using external stimulation suddenly could cause a collapse of his main body’s condition.

Ba Er had no choice but to suppress the urge.

When Fat Ball heard this question, it suddenly fell silent.

Had Ba Er’s words struck a weak spot in its heart?

After a long pause.

“I don’t know,” Fat Ball said.

Ba Er: “!!!”

“My memories split from those of the Heavenly Dao ball after the fight with the Sage of Confucianism ended. But if I trace back further, my memories... only involve cultivation, meditation, learning, cultivation...” Fat Ball explained slowly.

Apart from a vast amount of knowledge and cultivation techniques, it had no memories of its own origins.

“Did the Heavenly Dao ball tamper with you?” Ba Er guessed instinctively.

It seemed that every generation’s Heavenly Dao had a habit of tampering with its corresponding ruler of the Netherworld.

The three-eyed young senior seemed very dissatisfied with his own Heavenly Dao and had mentioned topics like ‘treat one’s own ruler of the Netherworld well’ during his exchanges with Song Shuhang.

Father Goudan had it relatively good; although researched by the Heavenly Dao, the Heavenly Dao truly cherished Father Goudan.

The ruler of the Dark Sun of the Netherworld Realm had their main consciousness synchronized and was directly seized by the Heavenly Dao’s countermeasure.

Senior White Two had his thigh cut off.

Now, it seemed like Fat Ball’s memories might have been tampered with by the Heavenly Dao ball.

“That big idiot!” Fat Ball, reminded by Ba Er, also thought of this possibility and was furiously enraged.

[Or perhaps, there’s something inherently problematic with Fat Ball’s origin?] Ba Er had another possibility in mind, which he didn’t voice.

Both guesses were plausible.

And deep down, Ba Er leaned more towards the second guess.

[First, I’ll report back to the main body and see if I can borrow Daozi’s ‘Heavenly Dao Authority’ later to perform some calculations and deduce information about Fat Ball,] Ba Er fed back this thought.

Ba Er packaged his two speculations about the fat ball and fed them back to his main body.

However, since his main body was currently in a multithreading spiritual debate state, Ba Er anticipated a delay in the feedback. He would have to wait until his main body finished the one-on-one debate with the first wave of Immortals before it could be received.

Ba Er was in no rush since time flowed differently there compared to the main world. He reckoned it wouldn’t be long in the main world before it all ended there.

“So, farewell, fat ball,” Ba Er said as he stretched lazily and stood up.

The eye that the fat ball had manifested glanced at him and then returned to silence—as if the irate fat ball from before was not the same entity.

Ba Er got up, leaving a dashing backdrop for the fat ball, and gradually walked away.

He knew the fat ball had not given up on self-rescue.

Once he left, the fat ball would surely continue to grind at the ‘Heavenly Dao Seal.’

Truthfully, Ba Er thought the fat ball’s will to survive was much stronger than that of his main body, Song Shuhang.

Now, even though it was suppressed and sealed by Daozi Senior, the fat ball still hadn’t given up hope—this character of the fat ball was such that as long as it persevered, given time and opportunity, it would certainly achieve great things.

Unfortunately... the fat ball’s luck had always been poor, time had always been biased against it, and it never seemed to have enough of it.

[Without the fat ball around, Senior White might feel a bit lonely, right?]

[However, after merging with Dark Song, it can also be seen as an alternative way of preserving a trace of the fat ball’s existence in this world. Moreover, Dark Song will only merge with most of the fat ball, not all. Perhaps it could leave some residue behind?]

Ba Er thought this as he stylishly walked away.

As he was pondering the term ‘fat ball,’ he accidentally triggered a hidden program within the Cultivator Chat System.

[Ding~ Message from the Cultivator Chat System backend: ????]

Ba Er: “???”

What on earth is the Cultivator Chat System backend message?

Oh... wait, could it be Lady Kunna?

Lady Kunna was currently busy upgrading functions for the Cultivator Chat System, so swamped that she couldn’t even find time to chat casually in chat groups. Now, she was sending messages directly from the backend without even switching from the upgrade interface.

“What happened, Lady Kunna?” Ba Er asked.

Lady Kunna: “Please call me Lady Fat Ball.”

Ba Er: “...”

Lady Kunna: “You keep thinking of me, are you thinking about me?”

Ba Er: “No, I was talking about the fat ball.”

Lady Kunna: “I am the Fat Ball.”

Ba Er: “...”

Heaven knows why Lady Kunna suddenly fancied the name ‘Fat Ball’?

Could it be influenced by that time the main body brought the seed influenced by pregnancy and the Embryonic Gaze into the Black Dragon World?

After sighing, Ba Er explained, “I just met the ruler of the Netherworld, the fat ball, the ball of liquid metal in the current world. Then, I was contemplating the origins of the fat ball, discussing this issue with him. Perhaps while pondering over it, I thought of the term ‘fat ball’ several times in my mind.”

Lady Kunna: “Oh, that one.”

After that ‘oh’, Lady Kunna did not reply further.

Ba Er: “...”

He was still expecting further conversation from Lady Kunna, but suddenly, the conversation just ended.

“Understandable, have to be understanding,” Ba Er said.

After all, Lady Kunna was very busy.

She probably couldn’t even spare the time to say ‘goodbye.’

The main reason is... the main body upgraded too fast, and the “Cultivator Chat System” also had to work overtime tirelessly to upgrade.

Lady Kunna had to compress tasks of at least a few thousand years or even tens of thousands of years into half a year. So, as you can imagine, her workload was terrifying!

That’s why Ba Er could understand Lady Kunna.

“By the way, speaking of Lady Fat Ball’s origins... I suddenly remembered why I like this name,” Lady Kunna suddenly replied.

Ba Er: “???”

Lady Kunna: “Fat Ball, it’s tasty.

Ba Er: “...”

Although Lady Fat Ball looks like a dango, it’s clearly metallic and doesn’t seem like it could be used as food.

And Lady Kunna, when did you eat Lady Fat Ball?

Could it be that Lady Kunna secretly made delicious food behind the main body’s back and quietly ate it alone?

Lady Kunna: “The memories are too distant. Moreover, my state has been affected by the collapse of the world, and many things have been sealed in the depths of the vast Memory Bank.”

“Too distant?” Ba Er was stunned, and suddenly he guessed a possibility, “Lady Kunna, did you eat Lady Fat Ball a long, long time ago, in the Black Dragon World?”

The origins of Lady Fat Ball are unknown to everyone and are not part of the current myriad practitioners in the universe... Could it be that it is a product of the Black Dragon World?

In the Black Dragon World, those who reach the Ninth Stage are blessed by the Black Dragon World and sent out of it. Could Lady Fat Ball be one of them?

Furthermore, Lady Kunna likes to call itself ‘Fat Ball’, there must be some karmic relationship here.

If one dares to think even bolder.

Could Fat Ball have once been a part of ‘Lady Kunna’?

But when Demon Emperor Hezhi was tampering with ‘Dragon Network’s Will of Black Dragon World’, did this part escape from the Black Dragon World, come to the main world, and eventually become Lady Fat Ball?

Every being at the Immortal level is a fantasist—they think too fast, imagining a lot of plots in the blink of an eye.

“Not in the Black Dragon World, but even longer ago,” Lady Kunna suddenly switched to ‘backstage mode’, entered the ‘Cultivate Chat System’ chat interface, and chatted with Ba Er.

Ba Er: “Longer ago?”

“The eighth session, it should be the eighth session... was the ball. And I should be the ninth session, I’m not wrong about that,” replied Lady Kunna.

Ba Er: “!!!”

What’s this ‘eighth session’?

Heavenly Dao?

And could it be a coincidence that Lady Fat Ball corresponds to the ‘Heavenly Dao ball’ of the eighth session?

“Request: please return to the Netherworld’s Fat Ball location, share your vision, I wish to take a look at the Netherworld’s Fat Ball,” said Lady Kunna again.

“No problem, I’m heading back to visit Lady Fat Ball right now,” Ba Er hurriedly said.

It feels like Lady Kunna is about to bring him some explosive news!

Ba Er turned swiftly, running back to the location where Lady Fat Ball was being suppressed.

Lady Fat Ball: “...”

Watching Ba Er return, it silently put away its means of breaking the seal.

“Hold on, Lady Fat Ball, I’m starting a video, haha,” Ba Er kindly said.

Lady Fat Ball, in a burst of rage, extended a pair of metallic arms and hammered at the seal: “I’ll kill you!”

Do they think it’s a monkey in a zoo?

.

.

Three thousand chapters check-in~~ Finally, the story of “Cultivator Chat” is also about to end~~

Chapter 3003: Chapter 3001: It’s Self-Protection for Children to Resemble Their Parents!

They’re actually video recording this—it’s as if they’re treating it like an animal penned up in a zoo.

And to top it off, they don’t even pay for photos!

Lady Fat Ball’s temper flared up uncontrollably.

Had it not been for the seal suppressing her right now, she would have flattened Thrice Reckless Mad Saber’s three corpses avatar under her massive form in a minute, rolling back and forth over him until he turned into a paper-thin figure!

In this world right now, she detests Netherly White the most, followed closely by Tyrannical Song—these two individuals always manage to rile her up with ease.

Despite Lady Fat Ball’s status and self-control acquired from her cultivation, she would usually not lose her temper so easily. But Song and White always seemed to carry a ‘provoking-the-ball aura,’ effortlessly triggering Lady Fat Ball’s fury inadvertently.

“Stay calm, Lady Fat Ball, you need to cool down for a moment. Anyway, no matter how angry you get now, you can’t hit me,” Ba Er said with a voice.

At the same time, his eyes lit up as he began to share his sight with Lady Kunna—the details of how the ‘sight-sharing spell’ worked were a mystery to him; he just needed to cooperate and open permissions, and Lady Kunna would handle the rest of the ‘sight-sharing’ operations.

Lady Fat Ball: “!!!”

Don’t think that just because you can’t be hit, you can do whatever you want.

Here, this is the Netherworld Realm.

And even though I’m sealed, I’m still the ruler of the Netherworld!

Lady Fat Ball calmed down and said with an icy, unemotional mechanical voice, “As the ruler of the Netherworld, I curse you... You will die without a whole corpse, your head blown to bits.”

“Uh, that’s basic for the main body, right?” Ba Er winked at Lady Fat Ball, “Ever since my main body started cultivating, I’ve lost count of the number of times it has exploded into a bloody mist. And there have been plenty of times my head has popped too.”

Lady Fat Ball: “...”

She turned her spherical body around, her materialized single eye now focusing on a figure above the ‘Demon Sea World.’

Her curse had just been neutralized.

By Dark Song...

The other party also has the authority of the ruler of the Netherworld.

This infuriating act of mutual negation reminded her of her past experiences of clashing and killing with Netherly White over tens of thousands of years. Such reflections only fueled her anger further.

Even though I am the ruler of this session’s Netherworld Realm, with Netherly White occupying the spot and Dark Song hastening to take a higher position, I still haven’t fully faded away!

Frustrated to the point of almost developing cirrhosis, Lady Fat Ball ultimately decided to close her single eye and even shut off her senses to the outside world.

Out of sight, out of mind.

She began focusing solely on countering the seal, wholeheartedly calculating methods to break the sealing technique.

As for the Thrice Reckless Mad Saber’s three corpses avatar nearby—let’s just treat him as a monkey jumping up and down!

...

...

“She isolated herself?” Ba Er sat down cross-legged, eyes fixed on Lady Fat Ball, transmitting the video feed to Lady Kunna.

“Yes, exactly as expected,” Lady Kunna said.

A thought struck Ba Er; he sat upright, preparing himself for Lady Kunna’s lesson.

“Although its color has changed, and its appearance somewhat altered, it still looks rather appetizing,” Lady Kunna said.

Ba Er: “...”

Truth be told, he just couldn’t associate Lady Fat Ball in front of him with ‘appetizing.’

“Back in the Black Dragon World, when I came into contact with the ‘seed’ that Tyrannical Song had brought over, I may have already subconsciously sensed and grown fond of the name Fat Ball,” Lady Kunna continued.

Ba Er: “So, Lady Kunna, could you explain the matter from beginning to end?”

“I don’t have time for that, I need to go back and upgrade the communication program,” replied Lady Kunna.

Ba Er: “!!!”

Suddenly, Ba Er felt moved by Lady Kunna’s dedication... She’s so diligent.

“Do you also want to eat the ‘fat ball’?” Lady Kunna suddenly asked.

Ba Er: “It’s not about eating, should it be about Fusion?”

“Isn’t that just another form of eating?” said Lady Kunna.

Ba Er: “Well... from a certain perspective, it’s indeed not much different. Lady Kunna, have you ever ‘eaten’ a being similar to the fat ball Senior? One that was also the ruler of the Netherworld?”

“Our counterpart was the Ancient Nether Chaos Will,” explained Lady Kunna.

Ba Er nodded: “Anyway, they are similar existences.”

After thinking for a moment, he cleverly said: “Lady Fat Ball, could you say a few more words?”

It seems that Lady Kunna quite likes the nickname ‘Lady Fat Ball’?

“Then, I will talk a bit more during my lunch break,” said Lady Kunna, her mood seemingly blossoming: “I, or to be more precise, the ‘me’ from before, or you could say my main body, was the last immortal body of a destroyed World, the ninth one.”

This information, Ba Er already knew.

Mainly because when looking at the Black Dragon World equivalent of the ‘Ancient Ghost’ big shots’ inserted pillars, Heavenly Dao Father Goudan’s father had left spoilers on those pillars.

So, Song Shuhang knew that the Black Dragon World is the relic of the ‘previous destroyed World’... The immortal Black Dragon was willing to let a batch of living beings survive, but at a certain cost.

And Lady Kunna is the will manifestation of the Black Dragon, the will of the Black Dragon World’s ‘Dragon Network’.

“Before me was the eighth one, which was also a ball... a plump one. According to the memory data in my Memory Bank, I had once entered the Ancient Nether alone, inserted the ‘Dao Mark Pillar’, and encountered the ball there. Then... I ate part of it,” Lady Kunna replied.

Ba Er: “Lady Fat Ball, you really have an appetite. What about the leftovers?”

“There were no leftovers. After eating a part of it, the rest just dissipated. Until later on, my counterpart ‘Ancient Ghost Will Body’ appeared... But because it looked so much like me, I couldn’t bring myself to do it,” Lady Kunna continued, pulling data from her ‘Memory Bank’ as she spoke.

Ba Er: “...”

So it seems, children resembling their parents indeed makes sense, for the more similar they are, the more protection they receive.

If the Ancient Nether Chaos Will hadn’t resembled its main body so closely, it might have ended up as Lady Kunna’s meal... and it might have been one of those things that she could harvest over and over again, regrowing to be eaten repeatedly.

“Eating the ball before becoming immortal would provide a lot of useful information... However, my Memory Bank data is a bit incomplete, so when exactly will you eat the ball?” Lady Kunna inquired.

Or should they consider consuming it piece by piece?

“Lady Kunna, did you eat the ball from the Ancient Nether before proving your Dao?” Song Shuhang was taken aback.

So, in the Black Dragon World era, after the eighth ball ceased to be, the ‘ball’ from the Ancient Nether was still alive, sort of like Senior White two?

What has happened in the past, will happen again... Is that what it means?

Moreover, Ba Er was more concerned about another point.

“Lady Fat Ball, is there any connection between the current fat ball Senior and the Ancient Ghost Ball you ate back then?” Ba Er asked.

Could it be that the successor of the previous eighth session, through Lady Kunna, secretly made its way to the main world to prove its Dao again?

But if it was the plan of the previous ball, after transforming into Lady Fat Ball, why doesn’t it remember its past?

Is it the price of going through destruction?

“Definitely,” replied Lady Kunna.

There’s definitely a connection between the two from the eighth session.

Chapter 3004: Chapter 3002: The Plan to Bind the Sage’s Eye Requires External Assistance

“p>”So, you mean... it turns out that the fat ball’s real body indeed smuggled itself from the Black Dragon World to the main world where we are now, and then proved its Dao during the Eighth Session?” Tyrant Evil speculated aloud.

“There might be that possibility. Besides having devoured the Ancient Ghost Ball in the past, I do not have too much understanding of the Eighth Session. Maybe it really had the means to smuggle itself successfully,” Lady Kunna thought for a moment and then added, “But I have another guess.”

Tyrant Evil thought briefly and said aloud, “Is it related to the ‘Eighth Session’ too?”

“Exactly,” Lady Kunna responded by nodding, “Two balls, both appearing in the position of the Eighth Session. It’s too much of a coincidence. Therefore, I am wondering if it could be that whenever the Eighth Session arrives... a ball might be born to mark the occasion?”

Because if the ‘fat ball’ in front of them was truly the one from her Black Dragon World that had smuggled over, then why would it choose to prove its Dao only during the Eighth Session?

Timewise, if it was truly a smuggled ball, then it should have been able to prove its Dao during the second, third, or fourth sessions.

So... could it be that every time the Eighth Session of the Will of the Heavens arrives, a ‘ball’ like this is born between Heaven and Earth?

Tyrant Evil had come to the same conclusion.

“Indeed, if it were a smuggled ball, surely it would avoid the first session of the Will of the Heavens. The first session is too special; as a smuggler, it definitely could not touch it. Thus, theoretically speaking, it should have chosen one session among the second, third, or fourth... holy shit...” As he said this, Tyrant Evil couldn’t help but tear apart the ‘seal of civility’ over his mouth.

The Will of the Heavens from the second and third sessions were the three-eyed young senior and Father Goudan, definitely unrelated to the smuggled ball.

During the fourth and fifth sessions, one of them was the main body of the ‘Dark Sun’...

When Tyrant Evil thought of this, he suddenly felt a tingling sensation on his scalp.

He immediately sent his speculations to his main body, as well as Daoist Senior.

“Don’t worry, this possibility is slim.” After a moment, the voice of Daozi rang in Tyrant Evil’s ear, “When I made contact with the Dark Sun, I discovered that it didn’t recognize the liquid metal ball at all. It even mistook me for the ball Will of the Heavens, and even thought of tempting me, trying to recruit me. So, there should be no connection between the two.”

Upon receiving Daoist Senior’s response, Tyrant Evil breathed a sigh of relief.

“However, I never thought the ball Will of the Heavens would be so special. If it really is born corresponding to the Eighth Session... what would its purpose be? Does the world need a ball to be born during the Eighth Session to complete something?” Daozi frowned.

Lady Kunna, “To be eaten?”

Tyrant Evil, “...”

“Maybe, it really is meant to be eaten.” After being silent for a moment, Daozi surprisingly agreed with Lady Kunna’s suggestion.

Saying this with his status as the current Will of the Heavens would not be without cause.

“We have been thinking about letting Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song’s Dark Song swallow the Netherworld Ruler Fat Ball, it might be a coincidence, but we are on the right path,” Daozi’s intent grazed the self-closed fat ball, feeling pleasure +1.

At the same time, Daozi happily reinforced the seal on the self-closed fat ball.

To enable Dark Song to fuse with the fat ball sooner... it would be necessary to accelerate the ‘inheritance of the Sage’s talent’ plan.

Daozi felt somewhat impatient.

“By the way, Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song... regarding the topic of ‘how to fuse your teacher’s eyes,’ we have a lead here, but it would require the help of a fellow friend,” Daozi’s voice sounded.

Tyrant Evil asked in confusion, “Who?”

So many powerhouses like Daoist Senior, Senior White, and Father Goudan had joined hands; did they still need to call for external assistance?

How remarkable could this reinforcement be?

“The Nine Nether Body of the Second Wielder of the Will, Senior Three-Eyed,” Daozi explained, “This suggestion came from Senior Dragon. In the myriad practitioners in the universe, no one surpasses the research pertaining to ‘eyeballs’ of the Second Will. Thus, the most reliable plan to solve the issue of ‘fusing the Sage’s eye and making a one-time-use item into something recyclable’ swiftly would be to have the Second Will’s Nine Nether Body help us.”

“I see, then I’ll inform Tyrant Kindness. He’s just gone with Self-Corpse Overlord to visit the three-eyed young senior to pick up Demon Emperor Og, so he can ask whether the three-eyed young senior would be willing to come out of retirement,” Tyrant Evil nodded.

...

In the small world behind the Throne of Wealth Distribution.

The trial area of the ‘Celestial Killing Light’ belonging to the three-eyed young senior.

The Demon Emperor Og had a face full of despair.

At this point, his situation could be described as utterly miserable.

With the seal of the Scholarly Sage, the backlash from the power of the Demon Sea World, the aftereffects of the burst techniques used in desperation, and the injuries inflicted by Tyrannical Song, he, who was already at death’s door, now had to withstand the relentless bombardment of the ‘Celestial Killing Light.’

It was too painful.

In the past few days, he had been constantly reflecting on his life.

Before he ascended to ‘Immortal,’ his life was like pushing through obstacles on easy mode, crushing all impediments with his overwhelming strength.

But ever since he encountered the Scholarly Sage and Tyrannical Song, his life plummeted like a stock market crash.

[After you guys finished your bet, why didn’t you remember to take me, the bet, out of there?]

[I’m going to die, I’m really going to die.]

[I, the mighty Immortality Demon Emperor, am going to die within the Immortal Slaying Thunder Pond? And my cause of death is because two gamblers fighting their corner forgot about their bet, me?]

At this time, whoever comes to rescue me, I will definitely fulfill one of their wishes!

Just when the Demon Emperor Og was in the depths of despair, two figures appeared in front of him.

One was Tyrant Kindness, and the other was Tyrannical Song with no presence, who would be forgotten in the blink of an eye.

“The Ancient Three Corpses Cutting Technique?” The Demon Emperor Og was startled.

He didn’t expect that Tyrannical Song would also play with the ‘cut three corpses’ method.

“Do you want to get out of this thunder pond?” Tyrant Kindness joined his hands together, looking at Demon Emperor Og with a compassionate face.

Demon Emperor Og: “...”

“The main body wants to hear about the ‘Mysterious Principles of Immortality’ from you. If you are willing, I can take you out,” said Tyrant Kindness.

“Do I even have a choice?” the Demon Emperor Og said with all the strength he could muster.

“Hmm, maybe you do have another choice,” said the Self-Corpse Overlord?. “Tyrant Kindness, I just received a message from Tyrant Evil. We need to meet with the three-eyed young senior again... And then, have one final gamble with him.”

If we win, we can ask the three-eyed young senior to help us with the project of ‘researching how to fuse the Scholarly Sage’s Eye with the undying fat whale golden core.’

It was the last gamble of the Throne of Wealth Distribution.

Tyrant? said to Demon Emperor Og: “You can become our bet once again.”

Demon Emperor Og: “???”

F*ck, you guys are doing this again?

There’s no end to this, is there?

“Got it.” Tyrant Kindness picked up Demon Emperor Og and, together with Tyrant?, left the thunder pond.

In the small world of the Throne of Wealth Distribution.

The three-eyed young senior lay on the beach wearing swimming trunks.

“Senior... let’s have the last bet. Can we stand in for the main body and do it?” Tyrant Kindness called from afar.

Chapter 3005: Chapter 3003: From Today Onwards, Tyrannical Song is My Bro!

“What are you planning to pluck from me this time?” the three-eyed young senior asked without turning around, responding languidly.

Tyrant Kindness: “???”

So devoid of spirit, this isn’t the three-eyed young senior I know!

In Tyrannical Song’s view, the three-eyed young senior was always more determined after setbacks, and no matter how many times he lost, he would come back with renewed confidence next time.

But the three-eyed young senior in front of him seemed like someone had replaced him... absolutely devoid of any spirit.

“Senior Three-Eyed, what’s wrong with you?” Tyrant Kindness asked cautiously.

“Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song, don’t worry, the master is just having his period~” the eyeball butler came out carrying the tea, serving the immortal tea to both Tyrant Kindness and Tyrant ? at the same time.

The three-eyed young senior: “...”

“His period?” Tyrant Kindness was taken aback.

The ruler of the Netherworld has such a setting?

“Senior, why don’t you have any fighting spirit?” Tyrant ? asked.

“But you? You show up punctually every month. Moreover, this time you didn’t even give me a month!”

“How do you expect me to have any spirit?”

An awkward expression appeared on Tyrant Kindness’s face—this was something he hadn’t considered.

Even the strongest person needs time to lick their wounds.

The main body has been shearing wool a bit too diligently.

“However, if you think about it, Senior, this is our last gamble with you. After this one, you can say goodbye to us. Thinking of it this way, doesn’t it make you a bit happier?” Tyrant Kindness said empathetically, trying to comfort from another perspective.

“Eh? Now that you mention it, it does make some sense.” the three-eyed young senior sat up from the beach.

He had almost forgotten, this was his last wager with Tyrannical Song!

After the ceremony, Tyrannical Song wouldn’t have the chance to sheer his wool anymore.

“Moreover, the main body isn’t here this time; we are clones, which should be a bit different from the main body,” Tyrant Kindness added.

The three-eyed young senior dusted the sand off his pants and stood up.

In the sky, the sunlight began to brighten.

The eyeball butler looked up at the dazzling sunlight—not very friendly for it. As an eyeball monster, it needed a lot of water, and too brilliant sunlight would evaporate the water content from its body.

Indeed, it’s the bloated mentality of the old master that should be fractured!

“Master, this is also your last chance to win against Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song... If you lose, your wagers with Tyrannical Song will be completely defeated without a single victory. Moreover, in the future, you will never have the chance to change this record again.” the eyeball butler kindly reminded.

The three-eyed young senior: “!!!”

The previously bright sunshine seemed to dim a little.

“Cough, what do you guys, the main body, want this time?” the three-eyed young senior coughed lightly and asked.

Given Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song’s character, he definitely wanted to get something from him, only then would he bother coming over.

Practically treating him as a treasure extraction vault.

“The main body has recently been studying a project, ‘Fusing a pair of Scholarly Sage’s Eyes into the undying fat whale golden core’, merging them into one entity.” Tyrant Kindness spoke up.

Self-Corpse Overlord continued, “In the process of research, we encountered some technical difficulties. We need someone to provide technical support for ‘eyeballs’... and Senior Three-Eyed, you are the senior with the deepest research on eyeballs in the myriad practitioners in the universe. Thus, we would like to ask you to assist in researching this project.”

Tyrant Kindness summarized, “This is the target of our bet, I wonder if you agree, Senior?”

“A pair of Scholarly Sage’s Eyes?” Upon hearing this, the three-eyed young senior felt a stir of excitement.

Was he being invited to research the ‘Sage’s Eye’?

This was problematic, the proposal had hit a soft spot in his heart.

The Scholarly Sage’s Eyes, Tyrannical Song surely wouldn’t use them as a betting stake and they were destined not to be added to his collection.

So it seemed the only way he could thoroughly study these divine eyes was by ‘assisting in the research.’

Such magnificent Sage’s Eyes, since they couldn’t be collected, touching and studying them also seemed wonderful.

So... should I intentionally lose this round to Tyrannical Song’s Three Corpses Avatar?

The three-eyed young senior began to struggle internally.

[And why does this have to be the goal of a bet? With our friendship, for such a minor matter, couldn’t he just invite me directly? Why go through the trouble?]

Seeing ‘a pair of Scholarly Sage’s Eyes’ as the prize, the three-eyed young senior secretly boosted his friendship value with Tyrannical Song by a lot- about five or six times the original, filling up his favorability to the brim.

“As a wager, would a living Demon Emperor suffice?” Self-Corpse Overlord pointed to Demon Emperor Og.

The three-eyed young senior: “...”

That felt rather dismissive.

But, considering ‘a pair of Scholarly Sage’s Eyes.’

“Agreed,” nodded the three-eyed young senior.

Demon Emperor Og: “...”

For a moment, he felt as if he had caught a whiff of disdain from the Heavenly Dao of the Three-Eyed Sovereign.

He, the mighty Immortality Demon Emperor, the big boss of demons, wasn’t even qualified to be a bet?

That felt awful.

“Then, Senior, how shall we proceed with this bet?” asked Tyrant Kindness.

“What are you good at?” The three-eyed young senior asked directly—having decided to lose on purpose, he thought to just go through the motions.

“What am I good at? Hmm, I am the Good Corpse of my main body, possessing countless good deeds and have inherited a part of the main body’s ‘Kindness.’ So, I am quite good at accumulating light of virtue, holy light, being a good person, and doing good deeds,” Tyrant Kindness honestly replied.

The three-eyed young senior once again showed an expression of disdain.

He originally thought of competing in what Tyrant Kindness was good at, but upon hearing these items, the three-eyed senior immediately dismissed the idea.

He, the sovereign ruler of the Netherworld, was supposed to compete in gathering holy light or virtue power?

Pah!

“What else are you good at?” The three-eyed young senior looked towards Tyrannical Song’s self-corpse.

Self-Corpse Overlord: “I excel at making people unable to remember me.”

“What’s your name?” asked the three-eyed young senior.

Self-Corpse: “Selfcentric Corpse Overlord Body.”

“That sounds pretty easy to remember,” the three-eyed young senior said. “Ba Ben.”

Self-Corpse: “...”

He was now the person who could most understand Drunk Fish Hermit from the Nine Provinces Number One Chat Group.

“Decided, this time, let’s compete in ‘memory,’” proposed the three-eyed young senior.

Chapter 3006: Chapter 3004: The Restless Butler

“”””Tyrant Kindness asked in confusion, “A contest of memory? How do we compare that?”

Under normal circumstances, cultivators have incredibly strong memories.

Having a photographic memory is something cultivators at the Second and Third Stage can achieve.

And when one reaches the Immortal Realm, the brain’s processing speed becomes indescribably fast.

Take Song Shuhang’s main body’s current state, for example, after sweeping through with his Immortal-level Primordial Spirit Power, he could encompass everything happening on modern world – Earth within his mental scan and perceive all things.

And everything that occurs within the range of the Primordial Spirit’s scan can be firmly remembered by the main body, down to the ruffling of leaves in the wind, without missing a single detail.

At the Immortal Realm, one could already do many things that are considered ‘divine’ in human myths, and even surpass most deities depicted in those myths, outperforming them beautifully.

If an Immortal so desires, they could ensure good weather, a life free from disasters and difficulties, and instantly receive and respond to the prayers of millions, all within their capabilities.

Hence, at a certain level, ordinary ‘memory contest projects’ would definitely be pointless.

Projects like random number memory, abstract images, or remembering people’s names and faces – for an existence at the Immortal Realm, one glance is enough to permanently remember everything, without missing anything.

Unless the competition is about who can first remember Fishing Hermit’s dao name?

However, if that’s the case, it might end in a draw.

...

...

“Mm, if we’re going to compete, we definitely can’t use ordinary tasks, let me think...” the three-eyed young senior stretched out his hands, and the eyeball butler came forward to drape a cloak over him.

The three-eyed young senior came to the side of Tyrant Kindness and Ba Ben, pulled out his own chair and lay down.

The eyeball butler then served the master immortal tea.

—Although it was always a pain in the master’s heart, contemplating switching jobs, duty calls where one serves, and professional responsibilities must be met. The butler could beautifully complete all the tasks required of him.

Tyrant Kindness watched the three-eyed young senior without blinking.

“I was thinking of using the Sealing Realm to add some fun to the contest. But now that you’re already at the Immortal Realm, sealing would be very troublesome... and it would also waste my precious materials,” the three-eyed young senior continued until he suddenly felt that the tea in his hand lost its flavor.

The last time he contended with Song Shuhang, this guy was still at the Eighth Stage Profound Sage.

This time, he has jumped to the Immortal Realm.

What about the normal Tribulation Transcender Realm?

Was the Tribulation Transcender Realm eaten?

Just thinking about this made the three-eyed young senior’s heart ache.

“Master, given Song Shuhang’s current realm, if we want to compete in memory, we must reach a limit with the ‘memory project’, surpassing what Immortal can accommodate,” the eyeball butler reminded from the side.

The three-eyed young senior rubbed his chin: “Hmm, like Song Shuhang’s last speech to the myriad practitioners in the universe, instantly replying to all cultivators’ questions and providing answers – then we see who can remember more of the questions and answers?”

The last time Song Shuhang suddenly connected to his database, the massive influx of information caused even his head to hurt.

The universe is vast, and the simultaneous questions from all cultivators in the universe almost caused the three-eyed young senior to crash.

“But now Song Shuhang has lost the qualifications to give a speech. He is no longer able to show his divinity in front of the masses and offer cultivators the chance to ask and receive answers,” the eyeball butler said, brewing some emotion and proposing: “So I think, why not extract all the memories of the master from the ancient era to the present and turn them into a competition project. The master’s memories from Eternity to now are so vast that even Immortals cannot instantly absorb and accommodate the amount of memory!”

First, the butler compliments the master, laying the groundwork.

“We can test whether Song Shuhang can memorize all of the ‘memories’ within a specified time. Then, based on the master’s memory, ask some random questions to see if Song Shuhang can answer them correctly.”

The butler spoke more and more enthusiastically.

“If the master really did this, then all of his memories would be laid out right before Tyrant Kindness, leaving no privacy between them,”

Just thinking about it felt very interesting.

The eyeball butler had even thought of a rough draft for the questions he would use to examine Tyrant Kindness.

For instance: how many eyeballs had the master, who had this peculiar love for eyes, collected in his lifetime?

Or: since the master started setting up gambling events, how many times had he lost? One could even delve into detail, asking who the master lost to in a given year and month?

And who was the master’s first love? What did his second love look like? What race was his third love, and how many pairs of eyes did they have?

At this point, the eyeball butler was becoming somewhat impatient.

“I think it could work,” Tyrant Kindness nodded – he was very interested in the three-eyed young senior’s memories as well.

Perhaps he could even catch a glimpse of the three-eyed young senior’s ‘Mysterious Principles of Immortality’?

“Keep dreaming,” the three-eyed young senior rolled his eyes three times.

He did not intend to make his memories public to anyone.

However, the proposal from the butler was not bad.

The three-eyed young senior’s gaze landed on ‘Gambling Demon Emperor,’ “How long have you lived?”

Demon Emperor Og: “...”

Is this targeting me?

I refuse to answer this question!

To become a bet was already inhumane enough, and now you even want to use my ‘memories’ as betting items, what more do you want to do to me before you’re satisfied?

You two demons!

No... both of the ones before me are rulers of the Netherworld.

To call them demons is practically a compliment to their kindness.

You two heartless rulers of the Netherworld!

“The ‘Gambling Demon Emperor’ and the Confucian Sage are from the same era, but he is much younger than the Sage...” Ba Ben chimed in from the side.

He remembered that the Gambling Demon Emperor, after proving his Dao and achieving immortality, couldn’t wait to challenge the Confucian Sage, but because he was too arrogant, he angered the Sage, was rubbed against the ground, and was even fitted with a permanent seal.

“So, he’s from the end of the ancient era? Too short, that duration of memories isn’t enough to be a wager for a bet,” the three-eyed young senior said dismissively.

Demon Emperor Og: “...”

Did I just get looked down upon again?

Why is there a feeling of loss deep inside although I don’t have to become part of the betting items anymore?

“Shall we use my main body’s memories as the wager? There are some things in the main body’s memories that are quite hard to remember,” Tyrant Kindness suggested aloud.

“No thanks, I have no interest in experiencing your memories,” the three-eyed young senior waved his hand dismissively.

He remembered that Tyrant Song’s mere one year of ‘Cultivation memories’ contained a lot of ‘Death Experiences, painful experiences.’ To touch these memories and try to remember them would be akin to self-torture.

The wise ruler of the Netherworld, having once been tricked by Tyrant Song’s ‘painful tolerance,’ would not fall into the same trap again.

“So, we might as well use the master’s memories. Master, you can edit your memories a bit,” the eyeball butler began to egg on.

Chapter 3007: Chapter 3005: The Original Ruler of the Netherworld’s Companion Item

A mature steward would never speak easily of giving up.

“Master, you can edit out some inconvenient private memories from your own memory, or even mix truth with falsehood by altering some scenes in your memories. After all, we just need a huge ‘memory’ as a wager,” the eyeball butler added.

It had already faintly sensed that its master was considering the suggestion.

With a little more covert encouragement, the deal would be sealed!

The three-eyed young senior crossed his arms and propped his chin, falling into deep thought.

Tyrant Kindness, Tyrannical Song’s Self Corpse, the eyeball butler, and the Gambling Demon Emperor all watched the three-eyed youth expectantly, waiting for his decision.

“Perhaps, I have something here that can serve as the object of this wager,” the three-eyed young senior said after a moment of thought, presenting an answer that surprised everyone.

After all this time, the three-eyed sovereign wasn’t planning to use his own Memory Bank?

The situation left the eyeball butler feeling somewhat downhearted.

“I have a Companion Magic Device that should be able to play a role at this time,” said the three-eyed young senior.

The eyeball butler was startled: “Master, you have a Companion Magic Device?”

Why didn’t I know anything about this at all?

How could the master’s little secret be hidden so well?

“I am the first ‘ruler of the Netherworld’ of the myriad practitioners in the universe; this is something I believe you should already know,” the three-eyed young senior stated as he gently tapped the vacuum, opening a small space treasure trove.

Tyrant Kindness looked up curiously into this little treasure trove... and the next moment, he was nearly blinded by its brilliance.

Song Shuhang had long known that the three-eyed young senior was extremely extravagant.

After all, only a person with mines at home could afford to wager so many precious materials and treasures and still host a Wealth Throne Ritual to distribute treasures to outsiders.

The treasures of grades 1 through 9 given away in previous Wealth Throne Rituals were no more than ‘garbage’ that the three-eyed young senior needed to clear out regularly!

Only the treasures he truly valued and collected were the real precious items.

Tyrant Kindness hardly recognized any of the precious treasures inside the treasure trove, each emitting an aura of inestimable value—and also, in one corner of the small treasure trove, there seemed to be many eyeballs, each carefully enclosed in exquisite treasure chests.

The three-eyed young senior retrieved a bottle shrouded in mist from the small space of his treasure trove.

Black, foulest mist continuously spilled from the bottle, then was reabsorbed—this cycle repeated endlessly.

“What is this?” asked the Self-Corpse Overlord Body, puzzled.

At the same time, he and Tyrant Kindness instinctively stepped back, their instincts warning them not to get too close to the bottle.

“This is the Companion Magic Device of my title as the first ‘ruler of the Netherworld’ in the myriad realms. To be precise, the fact that the corresponding Will of the Heavens created the ‘ruler of the Netherworld’ is also related to the prototype of this object,” the three-eyed young senior remarked with some emotion.

The first Wielder of the Will was very mysterious, erasing all information about itself... And furthermore, the first Wielder of the Will did not have a corresponding ‘ruler of the Netherworld.’

Before the appearance of the three-eyed sovereign, the Netherworld Realm was still the Primordial Demon Sea, utterly chaotic, without any rules.

It was only long after the Heavenly Dao’s Three Eyes rose to a higher position that it conceived of the ‘ruler of the Netherworld’ during an experiment.

After the Three-Eyed Youth created the ruler of the Netherworld, this existence was recognized within the laws of the Heavenly Dao, embedded into them, and passed down through the ages.

Essentially, every incarnation of the Heavenly Dao is a player who creates complications.

The Three-Eyed Youth actually shares some similarities with the Wielder of the Will Striped Dragon, both being outstanding inventive types of Heavenly Dao.

Heavenly Dao Eye Drops, the primordial treasure ‘Long-Eyed Orb Planet’, ruler of the Netherworld Realm... These are all works of the Three-Eyed Youth.

“What is its original form?” the Self-Corpse Overlord Body asked again.

The three-eyed young senior reached out and caressed the small bottle, then a single eye made of special material popped out from it.

The foul solitary eye landed in the palm of the three-eyed young senior and after a slight rotation, it locked onto the position of his third eye.

That was where it was meant to reside, in its socket.

“You are not unfamiliar with the origin of its original form,” the three-eyed young senior said, “It is that world which Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song referred to as the ‘special world’ of the Black Dragon World.”

Each iteration of the Heavenly Dao, or members who possess the qualifications to compete for the final battle for the Heavenly Dao, seemed to enter the Black Dragon World for some reason before proving their Dao and plant a pillar there.

The First Heavenly Dao, three-eyes, Striped Dragon Two, Demon Emperor Hezhi, Confucianism Sage... all have once left their marks there.

However, Demon Emperor Hezhi was a bit different; he entered the Black Dragon World after failing to compete for the Heavenly Dao.

“The Black Dragon World has a complete main world system, and there is a corresponding Ancient Nether World. In the Ancient Nether World, there exists a ‘Ancient Nether Will Collection.’ That may very well be the opportunity for my corresponding Heavenly Dao to tinker with the ‘ruler of the Netherworld Realm’ experiment,” the three-eyed young man explained.

However, the Ancient Nether Will Collection might have some defect due to ‘Heaven and Earth Defect’ or other reasons. From what we see now, it is not as complete as the ‘ruler of the Netherworld Realm’.

The ruler of the Netherworld appears to be an upgraded version of the ‘Ancient Nether Will Collection’.

“And this original form of my Companion Magic Device should be a treasure that my Heavenly Dao brought out from the ‘Ancient Nether’ of the Black Dragon World. After many experiments with that treasure, I was ultimately born in the Netherworld Realm,” the three-eyed young senior explained.

Unlike the later ruler of the Netherworld, when the three-eyed young senior was born, his corresponding ‘Heavenly Dao’s Three Eyes’ had already proved his Dao.

Therefore, the memories he inherited were different from those of the later ruler of the Netherworld, not split at the moment the ‘Heavenly Dao’s Three Eyes’ proved his Dao.

The Memory Bank of the three-eyed young senior retained some information about the actions after ‘Heavenly Dao’s Three Eyes’ proved his Dao.

However, later, as the Three-Eyed Heavenly Dao followed the example of the First Heavenly Dao, erasing its own information data, the information about the ‘Heavenly Dao’s Three Eyes’ in the Memory Bank of the three-eyed young senior was also disturbed.

Even his past ‘memories’ were actually affected.

During that time, to erase his information data like the First Heavenly Dao, the Three-Eyed Heavenly Dao conducted some excessive experiments on Eye Goo-goo in secret—just like what Wielder of the Will White did to Senior White two secretly.

These experiments, Eye Goo-goo had no recollection of, as they were done by the Heavenly Dao in secrecy.

But his Companion Magic Device recorded them all.

“In my Companion Magic Device, many memories are recorded... most of them related to me. They serve as perfect subjects for this betting contest,” the three-eyed young senior said.

“Isn’t that the same as your own Memory Bank, master?” the eyeball butler asked, confused.

“No, there are differences,” the three-eyed young senior waved his hand.

Then, he looked at Tyrant Kindness, “What do you think?”

“I will follow Senior’s arrangement,” Tyrant Kindness nodded in agreement.

Chapter 3008: Chapter 3006: Instincts About to Be Etched into Genetic Genes

“Alright, then you must do as I say. I’ll pick an auspicious day and find you a good household to marry into, so just wait peacefully to be married off,” the three-eyed young senior chuckled heartily.

Tyrant Kindness: “...”

“Master, that joke was so cold I’m starting to freeze up,” the eyeball butler muttered quietly.

As soon as it finished speaking, it was impaled to the ground by a casual spear thrown by the three-eyed young senior, and blood spilled all over the place.

The master’s temper has been growing worse and worse lately, he’d go straight to physically stabbing it in the heart over trivial things, which is too irritable... This isn’t good.

As an excellent butler, it felt it should find a way to adjust the master’s state and improve his irritable mood.

[Maybe dietary therapy would help.] The eyeball butler thought to itself, it needed to check what the ruler of the Netherworld could take to make it easier for him to fall asleep.

When a person becomes extremely drowsy, they begin to become lethargic, and even an irritable disposition can improve.

The three-eyed young senior cleared his throat and said, “Since you agree—”

“No, I won’t marry.” Tyrant Kindness hastily said.

Three-eyed young senior: “...”

I was joking before, but now I’m seriously discussing the issue!

“Shut up and listen to the rules of this trial,” the three-eyed young senior said.

Self-Corpse Overlord quickly covered Tyrant Kindness’s mouth—Senior Three-Eyes seemed in a really bad mood today, he might really be having his ‘time of the month’.

“The memory fragments stored in my Companion Magic Device are similarly vast, barely lesser than mine... And since it is not a biological being, its way of reading memories is different from ours, so the way it processes memories is also unlike us,” the three-eyed young senior began explaining.

His Companion Magic Device doesn’t remember things chronologically, it often starts with the beginning A, skips the middle sections C and D, and jumps directly to section E, but sometimes it unpredictably leaps back to section B from J.

To sum it up, it’s a total mess.

However, it obviously has a special program to read its memories, no matter how chaotic the memories are, it can neatly piece them together on its own.

Apart from itself, it’s extremely difficult for outsiders to read its memories, requiring not only the ability to read but also to piece memories together... Top-notch reading comprehension is a must.

Sometimes, you have to fill out the story with your imagination; sometimes you have to sort out the jumbled memory sequences; other times, you still have to delve deep into the Companion Magic Device’s psyche, to deduce the underlying meanings of its memories.

This undoubtedly added difficulty to Song Shuhang’s challenge.

Tyrant Kindness listened while nodding silently—this wasn’t too challenging for him.

His main body, Song Shuhang, enjoyed reading, particularly squatting in a rental bookshop to read.

Sometimes the books in the rental shop would be missing several volumes from a set, leaving gaps when he was reading.

Over time, his main body developed the ability to read books non-sequentially. Even if the order was flipped, starting with 1, 2, 5, then going back to fill in 3 and 4, it did not impede the reading experience.

And as the Three Corpses Avatar of the main body, he naturally inherited this foundational ability.

“Here are the rules of the competition: I give you half an hour to thoroughly absorb the memory content stored in the Companion Magic Device. After half an hour, I will extract 50 questions from the vast memory bank for you to answer,” the three-eyed young senior announced.

“How many correct answers count as passing?” Tyrant Kindness asked.

“Two points per question, get thirty correct for a passing score of sixty. If you answer all correctly, not only will I cooperate with you to study the ‘Scholarly Sage’s Eye’, but I will also give you an additional precious treasure,” the three-eyed young senior stated, tapping the armrest of his chair.

“What treasure?” Tyrant Kindness’s eyes gleamed.

“The details of an ‘immortality path’ that no one has practiced yet and where a seat of longevity still remains vacant,” said the three-eyed young senior. “Although you’ve already stepped onto the path of immortality, surely there must be others around you who would need such a complete ‘Will of the Heavens’ detail.”

Tyrant Kindness immediately thought of Senior White.

Only with the Scholarly Sage’s Eye complemented by an immortality path can one inherit the innate skills of the Sage.

Senior White would need to consume a path to immortality at that time.

“Full marks, it’s mine!” Tyrant Kindness declared with boundless bravado.

“Very good... that’s the spirit I want,” the three-eyed young senior chuckled.

What if Tyrannical Song doesn’t perform well and ends up losing to him?

Therefore, it is imperative to support Tyrannical Song, to ensure he wins this round and takes him to study the Sage’s eyeballs!

“Since you agree with the rules and the competition items, let’s sign the ritual now,” the three-eyed young senior urged while the iron was hot.

He couldn’t wait to study the Saint’s eyeballs.

“The ritual can be established at any time, my betting stake is a living immortal, gambling chips Demon Emperor Og!” Tyrant Kindness announced.

Demon Emperor Og: “...”

What the hell is a ‘gambling chips Demon Emperor’ title?

Is this really Tyrannical Song’s ‘Good Corpse’ manifestation?

Where’s the kindness?

Where’s the conscience?

Chapter 3009: Chapter 3007 “How the Ruler of the Netherworld Was Made
Innate instincts are something that cannot be forbidden, just like how ordinary people need to breathe.

Just a gentle touch from Tyrant Kindness’s hand on it had stirred its usually untroubled heart. Following that, it felt as if it had engaged in long-missed exercise and grappled with a formidable enemy, leaving it indescribably comfortable throughout.

Moreover, when the other’s fingers touched it, it sensed the continuous transmission of ‘kindness,’ as if the other was trying to curry favor.

Theoretically, as the Companion Magic Device of the ruler of the Netherworld and a symbol of the foulest evil, it should be highly resistant to ‘kindness.’

However, the kindness emanating from ‘Tyrant Kindness’ was something the Magic Device couldn’t refuse.

Just as godly weapons cannot refuse maintenance.

Godly weapons don’t need maintenance and can still cut through iron like mud... but after being maintained, they shine even more wonderfully.

Between the Three-Eyed Companion Magic Tool and Tyrant Kindness, a progress bar labeled ‘Friendship Value’ began to form.

And this progress bar started to steadily rise.

On the side.

In the sky of the Throne of Wealth Distribution’s small world, the sun suddenly shone bright and cheerful.

This brightness was different from splendor.

A splendid sun, like the scorching midsummer sun, makes one overheat, but this bright sunshine, like the winter sun, felt warm.

[Could it be the influence of the Companion Magic Device?] the three-eyed young senior looked at his Companion Magic Device, then at Tyrant Kindness’s hand that moved like it had ADHD, sometimes sliding and the fleeting brilliance that followed.

A moment later, the three-eyed young senior fell into meditation.

But even in a meditative state, his mood couldn’t stop brightening, as if he was bullying some little dragon years ago.

In the hands of the three-eyed young senior, there was more than one set of ‘complete Immortality Method Information.’

From the ancient era to the present, he had developed not just one ‘path to immortality’ theory, and while some had become useless because the geniuses of the main world had proved them, others had never been proved by anyone.

Giving away a set of ‘Immortality Method Information’ was still within his means.

Inside the memory space of the Companion Magic Device.

He fully activated his mental energy, went berserk to expand his range of mental energy, and wildly scanned the vast sea of memories.

As if sensing Tyrant Kindness’ fighting spirit, the Companion Magic Device, whose favorability was continuously rising, also felt moved.

Moments later, touched by his efforts, the Companion Magic Device decided to unlock and share a segment of its most treasured memory for the agreeable ‘Tyrant Kindness’ to inspect.

This is the great use of raising favorability!

After the Companion Magic Device made up its mind, it actively drew in Tyrant Kindness’ consciousness from the memory bank and brought him into the treasured memory area.

Just as Tyrant Kindness was going berserk and frantically scanning the memory area, something stirred within him.

“How the Ruler of the Netherworld was Forged”

Chapter 3010: Chapter 3008: Senior Three-Eyed: I Did My Best!

In the Netherworld Realm.

Chapter 3014: Chapter 3012: I’m Not Listening, I’m Not Listening

The fat ball stared at the approaching Tyrant Kindness.

Once upon a time, this little bug that it could crush hundreds of times at will had now grown into a significant existence that controlled its fate.

If there were such a thing as a regret medicine, if time could flow backward... it would definitely keep away from this little bug, not entangling with it at all. Or perhaps, it should have focused on crushing this annoying bug from the start, crushing it until it could not resurrect.

Either kill it or stay completely away.

Chapter 3016: Chapter 3014: Forced to Drop
