And for the secret appraisal technique, if it needs to appraise information involving the mysteries of Eternity or even the Black Dragon World, it’s unknown what kind of price must be paid. Even his Immortal Realm main body might not be able to withstand it.

“When the Heavenly Dao ball corresponding to me was collapsing, did it leave any clues? You could ask the scholar system’s Daozi to search for traces,” fat ball suggested at this time.

“I’ll report back to Daoist Senior,” said a voice from the vacuum, where an invisible reliable three corpses spoke.

Meanwhile, Tyrannical Kindness also said, “By the way, if your guess is correct, fat ball... it feels like your imposingness has dropped a lot.”

fat ball: “???”

“Every Heavenly Dao of various generations is almost always scheming something. Only the Heavenly Dao corresponding to you was being schemed against. Additionally, perhaps your main body was an experimental subject,” Tyrannical Kindness said.

The Heavenly Dao of fat ball does not fit in with the other Heavenly Dao at all.

Chapter 3017: Chapter 3015: How Can I Not Disgrace the Immortal’s Reputation?
At last, Fat Ball had discovered that besides piercing people’s hearts, Tyrant Kindness had a fatally tempting flaw—his train of thought made alarmingly huge leaps!

In the midst of a conversation, his thoughts would suddenly jump into an unknown ravine. Even when discussing critically important matters, his mind remained hyperactive, never focusing on one thing.

Such a person would definitely be unable to concentrate properly on their studies, eventually becoming one of the academic failures.

Moreover, this type of person would definitely be unable to seal themselves up for cultivation properly.

Not being able to seal up for cultivation meant they couldn’t cultivate properly, ultimately becoming a bottom-tier member of the cultivators...

Bullshit!

This guy had already, through sheer stubbornness, advanced to an Immortal!

Fat Ball sighed in distress.

This isn’t cultivation.

“Ba Xiu, has Senior Daozi sent back any message?” Tyrant Kindness suddenly turned and shouted into the vacuum—after his thoughts made a full loop, he surprisingly jumped back to the main topic!

“Senior Daozi is checking the records during his spare time, it will take some time,” Ba Star responded.

“Oh, then let’s contact the three-eyed young senior, and tell him the ‘companion magical treasure master’ has come out with us,” Tyrant Kindness lifted his hand to hold the companion magical treasure in his palm. With a few flickers in his right palm, he casually cast two Saber Nurturing Techniques.

Ba Star had a complicated expression: “...”

However, his consciousness, through the main body’s Throne of Wealth’s mark, began contacting the three-eyed young senior—handling the communication himself felt more reliable. Leaving it to Tyrant Kindness could lead to God knows what antics.

[Beep—Beep—Beep—The user you are calling is currently asleep and cannot be reached. Please try again after he wakes up.]

The gentle voice of the eyeball butler came from the Throne of Wealth’s mark.

Ba Star was stunned.

Wasn’t he just fine when we came out? Why did he suddenly go to sleep?

Do rulers of the Netherworld all have such good sleep quality, able to sleep whenever they want?

That’s a bit enviable—after reaching the Immortal Realm, the sensation of sleepiness basically disappears, and the function of sleeping degrades.

“What happened?” Tyrant Kindness asked.

“The three-eyed young senior is sleeping... Speaking of which, do all rulers of the Netherworld require a lot of sleep?” Ba Star said.

Tyrant Kindness answered, “They probably do. Senior White t-w-o often sleeps a lot too, the deep kind that you can’t wake him from even if you shout, making one unable to resist wanting to go up and...”

Boom—

Before he could finish speaking, a bolt of Netherworld Evil Thunder struck from the vacuum, exploding upon Tyrant Kindness’s body.

This was the Netherworld Realm.

Speaking ill of the ruler of the Netherworld behind his back in the Netherworld Realm would have consequences.

[Well done!]Qiu Youyou, upon seeing this scene, felt rather pleased—additionally, do all rulers of the Netherworld really need sleep? Could it be because I don’t sleep often that I don’t fit in with the other rulers of the Netherworld?

“I couldn’t resist... wanting to go up... and cover him with a blanket,” Tyrant Kindness cleverly changed his words after being struck by the lightning.

In the vacuum, the second bolt of Netherworld Evil Thunder that was gathering quietly dissipated.

Ba Star massaged his temples, “So, what were you about to say originally?”

“Don’t frame me,” Tyrant Kindness’s eyes continuously glanced towards the sky, signaling covertly.

“Let’s go, it’s time to report back to the main body,” Ba Star sighed, and then added, “Besides, bringing out the companion magical treasure might be a good thing.”

“Why would you say that?” Tyrant Kindness waved to Qiu Youyou, and then opened the gate to a ‘time-distorted secret realm.’

“If the companion magical treasure is in our hands, we can try to make the three-eyed young senior come out to retrieve this magical treasure... If the three-eyed young senior agrees, then we can set up a plan, hoping that when the three-eyed young senior comes to retrieve the companion magical treasure, he can come in contact with the ‘Sage’s Eyeball Research Project.’ If the senior shows interest in researching the Sage’s eyeballs, then our plan will succeed,” Ba Star spoke out.

Tyrant Kindness heard the words and praised, “Truly befitting of a self-corpse, the strategy is as excellent as the main body itself, with a black belly button and a dirty heart.”

...

...

World of the Throne of Wealth Distribution.

A sinister smile appeared on the face of the three-eyed young senior.

The ruler of the Netherworld, even a smile that came from the heart would turn sinister and terrifying under the influence of the aura of the Netherworld Realm... unless one’s appearance was incredibly outstanding, surpassing the influence of the Netherworld ruler’s aura.

“What was that self-corpse of Tyrannical Song called again? It has potential,” the three-eyed young senior said.

It perfectly coincided with his plans!

Much more promising than the other three corpses ‘Tyrant Kindness’.

Just a moment ago, when whatever-his-name-called-again phoned, the three-eyed young senior had intentionally ignored the call... His plan was to wait until Tyrannical Song’s three corpses approached the location of the ‘Confucian Sage Research Project’ and then return the call, finding an excuse to get involved with the Sage’s Eye research experiment.

Unexpectedly, the one on the other end had the same idea.

“This self-corpse of Tyrannical Song is fated with me! Later on, I’ll send him a way to immortality as a gift,” the three-eyed young senior happily said.

The eyeball butler beside him showed a content smile—although Tyrannical Song’s Three Corpses avatar lost the competition, it still received a reward as good as a ‘perfect score’.

A way to immortality, as well as the opportunity for the master to participate in the research of the Sage’s Eye.

Sometimes, it’s really not necessary to fuss over temporary gains and losses in winning or losing.

“Master, the special cement and Sealing Barrel are all prepared,” the eyeball butler said.

The three-eyed young senior cheerfully said, “Good, prepare a few more barrels... We’ll go find Tyrannical Song later. Oh, this time we might run into Father Goudan. Prepare a disgusting gift for him, as a meeting present.”

“How disgusting?” asked the eyeball butler.

“As disgusting as possible, and preferably not too valuable. If it’s too expensive, it’s like killing a thousand enemies while self-harming eight hundred—it wouldn’t be beautiful,” the three-eyed young senior said.

“Alright, master, I’ll definitely handle this properly for you,” the eyeball butler replied—he had an idea, planning to get a saber that would explode with the power of holy light, and a Seventh or Eighth Stage rank would suffice.

This way, after fully disgusting the Striped Dragon Ruler with the gift, it was likely that the Striped Dragon Ruler would carelessly toss it to Tyrannical Song.

Then, Tyrannical Song could pass this gift to his disciple who cultivated holy light.

This is called waste utilization.

...

...

Meanwhile, in the main world.

Tyrannical Song’s steel manifestation was worried.

It was the new year, and he also planned to give a few little guys some New Year’s gifts.

Last year, the main body Tyrannical Song had prepared some stuff—storage bottles obtained from celestials, as well as high-quality cosmos bags, Branded Wooden Sabers, and other trinkets.

When Tyrannical Song began preparing these gifts, he was still in the Fifth and Sixth Stage Realm.

Back then, giving these gifts to the younger ones was perfectly appropriate for him.

But now... he had become an Immortal big shot.

Would it be somewhat disgraceful for an Immortal big shot to give storage bottles, such low-tier items, to the younger ones during the New Year?

Chapter 3018: Chapter 3016: Little Guoguo, Your Path Has Narrowed
I’m having such a hard time, my main body is advancing too quickly, but my ability to amass wealth can’t keep up.

Sometimes, I finally obtain a batch of precious treasures from big shots like King Kun, but before I can even warm them up, they’re either spent in a Pay-To-Win Strike or used for upgrading my magical treasures... I can’t save anything.

My main body is such a spendthrift!

Although some treasures are left, like the Immortal parts and the like... I can’t give those to these little rascals.

Too powerful treasures, just their inherent Tribulation Transcender aura or Immortal Great Way aura, could harm these little guys.

Sigh~

“Senior Brother Song, is something the matter?” little Guoguo asked, puzzled.

Just now, Senior Brother Song Shuhang suddenly called all of us little guys together, seeming like he had something to tell us. But after he gathered us, Senior Brother Song started to space out, looking like he had something on his mind.

“Yes, I’ve prepared some New Year’s gifts for you guys.” The steel manifestation showed a gentle smile, took out several celestial race tiny bottles + Branded Wooden Saber, and handed them to the little ones.

Even little Li Yinzhu and the half-egg, half-human mechanical girl, who were playing with the little ones, got a set of New Year’s gifts.

——The disciples’ New Year’s gifts would have to wait a little longer, the main body had long made extensive preparations for the disciples’ gifts.

“Thank you, Senior Brother!” Loli Shi took the gifts happily and thanked him—she really liked these tiny bottles; these were magical treasures with an ‘inch-reducing purse’ function. Disciples from big sects like hers usually had to wait until they officially left the mountain to have a chance to get such storage-type treasures.

“You’re the best, Senior Brother.” Loli Zhu jumped happily and gave the steel manifestation a hug.

“These two gifts, I prepared for you half a year ago... Besides these, do you have any special New Year’s wishes?” the steel manifestation asked with a smile.

——This was the best solution he could think of!

As an Immortal-ranked steel manifestation, he had the power to promise these little ones a ‘New Year’s wish.’

Whether it’s soaring through the skies or diving deep into the oceans for shrimp, it’s not a problem.

As long as it’s not an absurd wish, it wouldn’t be too difficult for the steel manifestation to fulfill.

I, the steel manifestation, am indeed the most intelligent of them all—among all the clones, only I am special; I’ve studied abroad!

The other manifestations just stayed by the main body’s side after being created and didn’t continue their studies.

Only I spent a long time studying abroad with the Heavenly Emperor’s Da Da Zi last year. During that time, I was also in a ‘no contact’ state with the main body, an experience that other greenhouse manifestations can’t boast of!

“A New Year’s wish? We can also make a New Year’s wish?” little Guoguo’s eyes lit up.

Perhaps it was because boys liked robots, but at this moment, little Guoguo felt that this steel-looking Senior Brother Song was simply too cool, even cooler than Senior Brother Song’s main body!

“Ah Song, any wish?” Yinzhu vigorously rubbed her eyes to wake herself up.

The steel manifestation indulgently stroked Yinzhu’s head and said, “You can tell me whatever wish you have, but I’m not Senior White, so there are some limitations.”

Senior White’s clone, who was eating dessert after a meal, blinked in surprise—why do I get dragged into this?

“Then, can I go first, Senior Brother Song?” little Guoguo cheerfully raised his hand; it seemed he had a wish ready.

The steel manifestation smiled and said, “Sure, little Guoguo, what’s your New Year’s wish? But remember, I will only fulfill one New Year’s wish for each of you, so think carefully and don’t waste the opportunity.”

Little Guoguo seemed to have grown up quite a bit over the past six months.

“I’ve always had a wish—when I become strong and a Seventh Stage Venerable, I want to spank Abbot Profound Principle in return, and make him unable to leave his bed for three days!” Little Guoguo said happily.

Steel manifestation: “...”

Silly child, I asked you to make a New Year’s wish, not to reveal your wildest ambitions!

“So, Senior Brother Song, my wish is, can I have the fighting power of a Seventh Stage Venerable for a short time?” Little Guoguo continued.

And then go and beat up Great Master Profound Principle? Little Guoguo’s New Year’s wish was actually well thought out!

“Silly Guoguo, you’re treading a narrow path,” sighed the steel manifestation—bragging so loudly, are you not afraid Great Master Profound Principle will hear you?

However, Little Guoguo hadn’t finished stating his wish, he continued to describe it: “Then, if I had the realm of a Seventh Stage Venerable, even for a short while, I could break the oath Abbot once made. He would be able to give up silent meditation and speak normally.”

Steel manifestation: “???”

This train of thought is truly worthy of a prospective member of the ‘Nine Provinces Number One Group.’

Furthermore, was Abbot Profound Principle’s diligent pursuit of silent meditation really related to an oath he made?

Curious, it turned its head to look at Senior White’s clone.

After a moment of recollection, Senior White’s clone said, “That was a long time ago... Great Master Profound Principle once accepted a disciple with good innate skill. Later, maybe because Great Master Profound Principle gave the wrong guidance in cultivation, or maybe the disciple was impatient and overeager, eventually there was an issue with the disciple’s cultivation. Since then, Great Master Profound Principle suddenly began to practice silent meditation.”

“And breaking the silent meditation is to mentor a disciple who reaches the Seventh Stage Venerables’ realm?” asked the steel manifestation in confusion.

Senior White’s clone shook his head: “I haven’t heard of that condition.”

“I’ve heard my senior brother mention, as long as one mentors a disciple who is stronger than oneself, Abbot could then speak normally,” Little Guoguo said earnestly. “So, if I have the power of a Seventh Stage for a short while, Abbot could speak human language, and we wouldn’t have to guess hard what he’s trying to say. Also, by the way, I could also... ahhh~ ah~”

Two powerful Vajra Fists pressed against Little Guoguo’s temples, lifting him by the force of the fists, as they vigorously gyrated.

Little Guoguo let out a series of screams.

“This scream, it somewhat resembles the ability of my main body,” the steel manifestation nodded in appraisal.

Senior White’s clone: “...”

Abbot Profound Principle’s iron fists bored in for a full half minute before putting Little Guoguo down, and then he rewarded him with a doting chop to the head.

Little Guoguo touched his head and looked dissatisfiedly at Abbot Profound Principle.

“The realm of power is something more reliable when self-cultivated... Although I have a way to let you experience the concept of the ‘Seventh Stage Venerable’ for a short period, you’d be wasted afterward,” the steel manifestation said with a smile, pressing down the lump on Little Guoguo’s head.

With the realm of an Immortal, it’s possible to directly inject energy into someone through certain sacrificial rituals, allowing them to experience the realm for a while. But once it is over, the recipient is basically ruined.

Little Guoguo’s face turned bitter upon hearing this.

“However, since your wish has been spoken, I should at least make a gesture,” said the steel manifestation, stretching out its palm, where formation runes began to flicker.

A moment later, a ball of lightning took shape in its palm, emerging...

Chapter 3019: Chapter 3017: Eh, who are you guys, why are you appearing in my mind?
This move is none other than Tyrannical Song’s strongest Lightning-based technique, the ‘Giant Heavenly Tribulation Lightning Palm,’ which even immortals from myriad practitioners in the universe dare not underestimate.

Based on the ‘Simplified Lightning Palm’ originally created by Senior White, Tyrannical Song incorporated his own understanding and enlightenment of ‘heavenly tribulation,’ ultimately concocting a Lightning Palm with the killing power of a heavenly tribulation.

Though the steel manifestation holds a Lightning Palm only the size of an apple in its hand, this is because the Lightning Palm hasn’t been released—once it is unleashed, it will be a Suppression-level Lightning Palm, with power at the Seventh Stage Realm.

The steel manifestation continues to maintain the ‘Suppression-level Lightning Palm’ in one hand while taking out some wood from the main world with the other.

Most of these were left over from the original ‘drowsy-eyed wooden body’ and are excellent materials for refining and manufacturing talismans.

The steel manifestation took out a strip of wood and whittled it into more than ten small wooden blocks the size of mahjong tiles.

Then, using the crude ‘Basic Sealing Skill,’ he forcefully sealed the Lightning Palm into the small wooden pieces by leveraging the pressure of his main body’s Immortal-level realm!

In the hands of an immortal, even the Basic Sealing Skill could perform wonders—the immortals are just that miraculous.

After properly sealing them, the steel manifestation nodded in satisfaction.

He then repeated the operation, sealing twelve ‘Suppression-level Lightning Palm’ mahjong-shaped formation tiles in one breath.

“Take these, these formation tiles can be released to allow you to withstand a head-on clash with a Seventh Stage Realm cultivator... However, the range of this technique is quite large, so be careful about the allies around you when releasing it. I’ve added a kind of smart technology that distinguishes enemies, but it relies on you to lock onto the targets.” The steel manifestation, who had studied abroad, mastered some very advanced techniques.

He had also shared these little techniques with his main body... but he didn’t know if his main body had mastered them.

“So many?” Little Guoguo carefully stored ten of the tiles into a ‘small bottle,’ and gave the remaining two to his friends, Loli Shi and Loli Zhu.

The older brother had taught him that good things should be shared with pretty little companions.

He considered giving one each to Xiao Lingxiao and little Li Yinzhu as well, but given that they were ‘daughters’ of Senior Brother Song, little Guoguo thought about it and felt it was unnecessary.

The little fellow has potential.

“Abbott~ from today onwards, I won’t let you slap my butt that easily anymore... I have grown up!” Little Guoguo shook the small bottle in his hand.

—A man grows up when he gains strength. Now that he has Senior Brother Song’s Lightning Talisman, does it mean he has acquired power? Could he also be considered as having grown up?

No sooner had he spoken than Great Master Profound Principle’s iron fist once again pressed against the little monk’s head and began to spin rapidly—this time, the spinning was so fast that the steel manifestation saw wisps of white smoke rising from the little monk’s head.

This time, the little monk didn’t even have a chance to scream...

The steel manifestation turned away, not looking at the small monk, and looked toward Shi and Zhu: “Then, do you two have any New Year’s wishes?”

Loli Shi, like a little adult, said seriously, “Senior Brother Song, I want to improve my mind and willpower.”

“Mind and willpower? Is your mind and willpower not stable?” wondered the steel manifestation, who thought that because of Shi’s composed nature, her mind and willpower were the most stable among the three little ones.

Loli Shi shook her head and said, “My mind and willpower currently match my realm... but I hope to possess an even stronger mind and willpower. I came into contact with Senior Brother Song very early. In addition to advancing quickly, brother also has a mind and willpower as stable as a rock, which always keeps up with his realm’s advancement. Therefore, I want to know the method by which Senior Brother Song keeps his mind and willpower so stable.”

Advancing quickly is indeed attractive, but without a matching mind and willpower, quick advancement becomes a hidden danger.

Loli Shi, seeming much like a little adult, thought things through very clearly.

Fairy Lychee, not far away, showed a satisfied smile. Loli Shi’s request for a New Year’s gift was very appropriate!

The steel manifestation slightly smiled: “If you asked about other cultivation matters... perhaps I really wouldn’t be able to give you a definitive answer. But if you’re asking about matters of the mind and willpower, you’ve indeed come to the right person.”

In addition to an exceptionally resilient constitution that allows him to withstand monsters, the main body, Tyrannical Song, also possesses an indomitably firm intent as well as a mind and willpower that even Inner Demons would steer clear of—these are also his main strengths!

Moreover, he does have a method suitable for low-grade cultivators to improve their ‘mind and willpower.’

The path of cultivation, the first step in tempering mind and willpower, is to endure solitude.

Within frustrating solitude, one forges the most basic, most robust mind and willpower—this is also why small cultivators like little Guoguo, despite their low realms, are assigned to sit in meditation for long stretches of time, even to the point of developing hemorrhoids.

“Senior Brother, Senior Brother Song, I want to make the same choice as Shi!” Loli Zhu called out, hanging from the neck of the steel manifestation, loudly.

Loli Zhu was the youngest and not as sensible, not thinking as much. But she knew, as long as it was Shi’s choice, following along would be good for her.

Because Shi was smarter than her.

“Alright, since you’ve made the same choice, I will give your New Year’s gift to you both,” the steel manifestation said with the kind smile that once belonged to Tyrannical Song.

The next moment, he reached out to touch his glabella, sending a report to his main body: requesting the use of the third eye.

In the blink of an eye.

The third eye condensed directly in the steel manifestation’s glabella.

“Prepare yourselves, the experience to come... will be unimaginably boring,” the steel manifestation said solemnly.

Shi nodded her head.

Seeing Shi nod, Zhu also nodded.

“Then... welcome to the beginning of three hundred years as an onion,” the steel manifestation spoke softly.

An “illusory reality” made up entirely of 0s and 1s unfolded around the steel manifestation, enveloping Shi and Zhu.

At the same time, from within the third eye, a light carrying a segment of Tyrannical Song’s memories shone upon Shi and Zhu.

It was the very scene of Tyrannical Song’s first experience tempering his mind and willpower—his experience entering the dreamland as Lady Onion!

The steel manifestation used the “illusory reality” and the “third eye’s forced information transmission” feature to emulate Tyrannical Song’s past experience entering the dreamland as Lady Onion.

Although Shi and Zhu were pulled into this ‘onion life experience’ project together, they were separately pulled into two different illusory worlds.

How could they have the opportunity to stay together if they are to truly experience loneliness?

Loneliness is to be savored alone, carefully.

In the world of illusionary dreams.

Shi and Zhu felt their bodies being held by a warm, large hand.

That hand held them as it climbed step by step to the mountain summit.

“Where is this place?” Shi asked, puzzled.

“Shi, Shi, where are you?” Zhu cried out in alarm from the neighboring illusory world.

“Success,” the steel manifestation thought to himself.

He had successfully recreated and replicated the detailed process of his main body’s original experience entering the dreamland as Lady Onion!

Now, Shi and Zhu had both become an onion lady without consciousness.

Both were planted by Daoist Priest Scarlet Heaven on the top of the mountain.

Next... enjoy the life of being an onion for hundreds of years!

The steel manifestation smiled kindly.

In the illusory world.

Shi and Zhu, just like Song Shuhang before them, endured the wind, the sun, and the rain on the mountain summit.

“Eh? Who are you guys? Why are you appearing in my mind?” suddenly, a crisp voice rang out separately in Shi’s and Zhu’s ears!

Chapter 3020: Chapter 3018: End Credits Easter Egg
Loli Shi and Loli Zhu, each in their own illusions, were both taken aback simultaneously.

Hadn’t Senior Brother Song said they should be prepared to experience profound loneliness? So why was there a pleasant voice sounding by their ears?

Could it still be called loneliness if someone was there to talk to?

And furthermore...

Shi felt that the voice sounded somewhat familiar.

But after carefully comparing it to the voices of fairies from her memory, she couldn’t find any that matched.

Could it be the voice of a fairy from her memories that had undergone some change?

However, if it was Senior Brother Song who had sent them into this world, then perhaps the appearing voice was also a part of the process to “stabilize Dao heart?”

At the very least, it shouldn’t harm her or Zhu.

With this in mind, Shi calmed down and replied, “My name is Shi... If you, Fairy, can sense another person, that should be my junior sister Zhu.”

But her voice did not reach the fairy.

“Not replying? Or can’t talk?” the crisp voice wondered aloud.

After a moment...

“Eh, is this entering a dream? Is it Boss Song’s dreamland skill?” the voice seemed to recall something.

[Boss Song?] Shi was stunned.

In her memory, the one who would call Senior Song that... wasn’t it Lady Onion, who often gets her head pinched?

On closer inspection, this crisp voice did indeed bear some resemblance to Lady Onion’s voice. But this crisp voice was more mature, like the difference between a young girl’s voice and a mature woman’s voice.

What had happened to Lady Onion? Her voice had changed so much, becoming so mature and tempting.

“Since when could your dreamland skill carry others along, Boss Song? You are too biased, aren’t you? You’ve never taken me along... Be careful, or I might double the staff’s salary this month?” the mature voice of Lady Onion continued, seemingly conversing with Mister Song.

Shi puzzledly sensed her surroundings, but she didn’t hear Senior Brother Song’s voice.

Could it be that Senior Brother Song was conversing with Lady Onion outside?

“But, since it’s because of Boss Song, then I won’t sever this karmic connection. You two little ones continue... I’ll give you a little Easter egg at the end.” The voice of Lady Onion grew fainter and ultimately disappeared.

[Such a strange feeling.] Shi thought, puzzled.

It felt as though Lady Onion’s voice was transmitting from a distant other world, as if crossing through time and space.

Furthermore... what about an Easter egg?

After the mature and tempting voice of Lady Onion vanished, the whole ‘onion life plot’ slowly unfolded.

This time, both Shi and Zhu clearly sensed that they had become onions planted in the soil.

[Is this the onion life Lady Onion mentioned?] Shi mused.

They could feel themselves turning into plants, roots planted deep in the soil, immobile, only able to sway with the wind.

At first, Loli Zhu found it refreshing and amusing—the experience of being an onion was completely different from that of a human, and she was having a blast.

But as day turned into night, and one day passed...

Even the most fun experience becomes tedious and boring without change.

Loli Zhu quickly grew weary of this onion life experience.

But... this was just the beginning.

The onions that they had become, swaying atop a mountain peak, were isolated; no one to talk to, no one else to interact with.

Daybreak, sunset.

Day after day.

Loli Zhu was starting to crack... it was too boring, especially for someone as lively and active as her, this mundane onion life was a terrible torture!

She was now beginning to regret following Shi’s choice to make the same decision; Shi’s personality might adapt to onion life, but it wasn’t for her!

Actually... even Loli Shi couldn’t bear it any longer.

No matter how mature, she was still just a child. At first, she could silently calculate the time in her heart and see how many days she had passed.

But after a few months, she was completely unable to calculate time anymore.

Her spirit had been tormented to the edge.

[After all, those motivational quotes are deceptive, being a carefree blade of grass on the vast prairie, swaying with the wind... Why don’t you try being a blade of grass?]

Besides, had Senior Brother Song ever experienced such an ordeal?

No wonder Senior Brother Song’s mind and willpower were so stable.

Such an inhumane life experience, so vividly felt, if one could endure to the end, how could their mind and willpower not be stable?

During this period, Shi and Zhu both thought about breaking Lady Onion to escape this extremely boring and tasteless world.

But... it couldn’t be done.

Song Shuhang had also thought about breaking his own onion waist to commit suicide and get out. However, the dreamland skill didn’t have this function.

One year passed, two years passed, ten years passed, thirty years passed...

Shi didn’t know how much longer she had to stay in this world. But there are some things. After enduring the most difficult times, one could actually start to slowly adapt.

As a disciple from a major sect, Shi had an excellent foundation in cultivation. Compared to Song Shuhang back then, she adapted a bit faster.

Moreover, deep in her heart, there was a thought—Senior Brother Song had persisted to the end, and she must persist to the end as well!

After calming herself down, Shi’s mind and willpower began to Reinforce slowly with the passing years of Onion life.

On Zhu’s end, she was almost forgetting she was once human, after all, her brief human life wasn’t as long as that of an onion... Being an onion, one must be determined to be an onion, absorbing nutrients from the soil, sprouting upwards, and through photosynthesis, serving all of humanity.

Shi, I don’t want to be human anymore!

Compared to the stable Shi, Zhu’s mentality was somewhat similar to Song Shuhang’s last year.

Then, a hundred years, two hundred years, three hundred years...

The mind and willpower of Shi and Zhu had been polished smooth.

While they were still waiting for a far longer Onion life, Lady Onion suddenly sprang out of the ground.

She sprang out?!

At this moment, Shi and Zhu were moved to tears.

Originally, they thought their current mind and willpower could remain unshaken even if the sky fell, but when Lady Onion finally sprang out of the ground, they couldn’t help but shed tears of liberation.

The world is still so beautiful!

The illusion plot came to an abrupt halt the moment Lady Onion sprang out.

The plot set by the steel manifestation was to let the two youngsters experience three hundred years of Onion life. The upcoming plot was not suitable for children.

Shi and Zhu are still children.

Even after three hundred years of Onion life...

“Is it over?” Shi sighed heavily.

She felt that her mentality was no longer young.

On Loli Zhu’s end, it was the same; she felt she could no longer be as naive as she was three hundred years ago.

Shi, I don’t want to be an onion anymore!

[Senior Brother Song had experienced such three hundred years, but he could still jump around lively without much change in his personality, and his mentality was still as young as before... Is this an innate skill, or is there some secret to it?] Shi wondered in her heart.

The ‘Dream Entry Plot’ had gone to a black screen.

We can finally go out, right?

Just as Shi and Zhu were thinking this, the world that had already gone to a black screen started to brighten up again.

It’s... still happening?

Chapter 3021: Chapter 3019: When in Doubt, Confront the Tycoon + Pain + Death
“The Dao heart that has been reinforced by three hundred years of green onion life is soulless!”

“Do you want to know the real reason why Boss Song’s Dao heart is so strong?”

“Let me open the gates to the world of the Dao heart for you!”

At this moment, Lady Onion’s mature and enticing voice echoed.

“No, I don’t need it. A soulless Dao heart is enough for me!” Loli Shi immediately refused.

To her, a Dao heart just needed to be strong enough to serve its purpose, so what did it matter if it lacked a soul?

But, just like before... her voice couldn’t be heard by Lady Onion.

After all, their experiences and Tyrannical Song’s true ‘dreamland skill’ were different.

Then, the mature and enticing voice of Lady Onion spoke again, “Soft Feather, dear, lend me your strength.”

“Soft Feather sister?” Shi was startled.

“Is Soft Feather sister going to help Lady Onion torment us too?” Zhu felt a pang of panic—Soft Feather’s personality was rare among fairies who could join in their play, making her an extremely dear playmate for Zhu.

If someone like Soft Feather sister were to assist Lady Onion, it would be terrifying.

The next moment, the darkened world flipped again and brightened up.

They were once again in possession of ‘Lady Onion’s’ body, but this time it was not the green onion itself, but Lady Onion with hands and long legs.

For some reason, even though the perspective should be first-person, both Shi and Zhu could ‘sense’ what Lady Onion looked like at the moment.

Her originally long green hair had been cut to a neat shoulder-length that made Lady Onion appear more mature, and she even had the air of a strong woman about her.

Her figure hadn’t changed much... because Lady Onion’s figure had always been quite Tyrannical.

But she seemed a bit taller?

And her attire had changed too, no longer the skirt of before but now a set of form-fitting trousers and high heels—truly the get-up of an elder sister figure.

“When did Lady Onion sister grow up to look like this?” Shi was surprised.

She had interacted with Lady Onion many times before.

And they had even played together.

Lady Onion’s character was such that she got along well with children.

However, this strong woman version of Lady Onion was completely unfamiliar to both Shi and Zhu.

“Here it comes!” the Lady Onion in the dream suddenly spoke in a deep voice.

It was the mature Lady Onion’s voice that Shi and Zhu heard.

In the next moment, an attack so terrifying that it defied description descended from the opposite vacuum.

When faced with such an attack, Shi and Zhu felt an indescribable terror welling up deep within them—an innate fear brought on by the overwhelming might of the attack, beyond their realm, suppressing them with dread.

There seemed to be several figures standing next to Lady Onion.

But since Lady Onion’s gaze wasn’t fixed on them, Shi and Zhu couldn’t see them clearly.

Boom~

The attack from the other side came crashing down like a flood.

It was darkness as tangible as solid substance, seeming like black light, yet also resembling some sort of virus-like thing.

Lady Onion stretched out her arms, and wings that resembled those of a phoenix spread from her back to shield herself and also to cover her companions beside her.

Then... Lady Onion perished.

She died a truly miserable death.

Just like a candle melting away.

First, her skin and flesh dissolved, followed by her bones and marrow...

In the blink of an eye, Lady Onion turned to ashes.

How tragic!

The dreamland skill active on Lady Onion, Shi and Zhu, was felt as though it were their own experience.

Such a deathly ordeal made their scalp tingle.

The kind of pain that shook the soul, along with the sense of powerlessness when facing the enemy’s attack, was like a red-hot branding iron, leaving a mark deep in their memories.

Unlike Song Shuhang, Shi and Zhu lacked the innate skill of ‘pain tolerance’.

The intense pain and the death experience knocked them out immediately.

Time passed, but they weren’t sure how long...

They opened their eyes.

Not dead yet?

“Pain... After resurrection, the pain still persists. Only Boss Song in the myriad practitioners in the universe could consider such pain as a part of his daily life,” the voice of the elder sister, Lady Onion, continued.

From the plot point of view, it seemed that Lady Onion and the others were resisting some powerful enemy?

Moreover, an enemy so powerful that they were unable to resist.

An enemy that could kill Lady Onion in one move.

Shi and Zhu clenched their teeth.

The memory of the pain they had faced before death still lingered in their minds.

The instant before they nearly died, every moment and every flash of the death process, and the endless darkness and despair after death, were deeply etched in their hearts.

Remembering the moment that had just passed, their souls were still trembling.

But in the end... they had made it through.

With the help of something like the ‘dreamland skill’ and the external interference from elder sister Lady Onion, they had pulled through.

It was the same principle as borrowing a CPU.

As long as they made it through, even if by relying on external support, the benefit to their mind and willpower was immense.

How did Tyrannical Song come to possess such a strong mind and willpower?

Especially in the later stages, when his realm was skyrocketing, why was his mind and willpower as stable as Mount Tai Seal?

Through pain, through death, by confronting powerful seniors!

He had tasted the pain that no one in the myriad practitioners in the universe could bear, and he had savored it.

Within one year, the number of times he died could rank in the top three in the myriad practitioners in the universe!

And that was quite a modest claim.

It was mainly because Cloud Gauze Three View Moon had a horrifying number of parts in the mountain of body parts, making it difficult to scrutinize her past highest number of deaths in a year...

Then there was confronting powerful seniors, opposing enemies that brought despair, which is also an extreme method to strengthen one’s inner self. Either under the pressure of a despairing enemy, one’s mind and willpower collapse, or one dares to directly face their strong enemies, enhancing the strength of their mind and willpower!

And Lady Onion left them an easter egg—confronting powerful seniors + pain + death, a one-stop service.

“Although I want to continue, unfortunately, if we keep going, you won’t be able to bear it. The foundation that three hundred years of living as a green onion provided is only enough for you to carefully go through this once.” The easter egg plot ended, and the voice of sister Lady Onion sounded.

The reason why an easter egg is called so, is because it’s just a brief few scenes, and not lengthy.

“My part is over, my dear friends, don’t forget to leave us a good review. Soft Feather dear, I’m leaving now,” Lady Onion continued.

“Mm,” the next moment, Soft Feather’s voice rang in Shi and Zhu’s ears.

Just as pleasant, but a voice that was different from sister Soft Feather today.

Shi had already vaguely guessed a possibility.

But she felt that this possibility was too shocking, theoretically impossible to achieve—the sister Lady Onion and sister Soft Feather in their ears didn’t seem to be from the time node they were in.

“Though it’s a pity... I cannot directly communicate with you, the fact that you, Shi and Zhu, are still safe and sound at this point in time proves that things are developing in a good direction,” Soft Feather’s voice slowly said.

Soft Feather had recognized their identity.

“Please tell Senior Song that our experiment here was a success. When consuming the ‘way to immortality,’ we can utilize the ‘small black room’ of the Will of the Heavens, a special space. In that forgotten world, where the source is erased. We can retain fragments of the way to immortality. Senior Song’s second way to immortality, by splitting and combining...” Soft Feather’s voice trailed off.

Shi and Zhu’s consciousness returned to the main world.

Chapter 3022: Chapter 3020: The Targeted Fat Ball

Loli Zhu, feeling as though she had lived for over three hundred years, quietly demoted ‘Sister Soft Feather’ to ‘Little Soft Feather’—she felt that the former Sister Soft Feather was now her little sister.

But the problem was... Soft Feather’s family name wasn’t ‘Soft’, and her given name wasn’t ‘Feather’.

The combination of Soft + Feather was just a traditional daoist method for creating dao names.

Sister Soft Feather remained Sister Soft Feather... a gap that not even three hundred years of onion life could bridge.

The inflated Zhu instantly came to terms with her reality.

Who knows where that stupid onion is now, how she is doing, if she has money for online shopping?

In the final scene of the dreamland Easter egg, the short-haired big sister Lady Onion had left a deep impression on her—she wanted to grow up to be like Sister Lady Onion, with a prominent front, a slim waist, and long legs.

The most important thing was—even in death, she had to die in an extremely cool manner.

Was this ‘Lady Onion’ really from his Tyrannical Song Group, the worker boss Lady Onion?

Our group’s worker boss Lady Onion couldn’t possibly be this cool!

Soft Feather was the only official member of the Nine Provinces Number One Group who addressed him as “senior”, so he counted her as part of the ‘give a New Year’s gift’ friends group.

She had many things she wanted to do, many places she wanted to explore, and now she had plenty of time!

Techniques like the ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’ and the ‘Sword-Nurturing Technique’ were actually not any profound lost martial techniques in the cultivation world.

Mechanical Girl Xiao Lingxiao: Σ(°△°|||)_

Is Sister Yinzhu planning to use the ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’ on her?

Is she not a cute little sister?

To take a portion to make a cloak for Xiao Lingxiao is also a good excuse to weaken Lady Fat Ball.

It’s not easy for cultivators to transfer techniques, but with the third eye, many memories can be transformed into data packages and sent out, like ‘copy and paste,’ which is especially convenient.

Meanwhile, in the time-distorted secret realm created by Daozi.

More than thirty days have already passed inside the realm!

Song Shuhang’s main body has been engaging in intellectual discourse with all the Immortal big shots non-stop, for a whole month now!

Most of the time, Song Shuhang has been listening. He had no choice; his cultivation-related theoretical knowledge wasn’t sufficient... After all, knowledge requires time to accumulate.

—Tyrannical Song’s theoretical knowledge might be lacking, but his realm is high. Plus, he is currently able to make use of Daozi’s ‘Heavenly Dao Calculator,’ which is like using the realm of the Heaven’s Will to listen to the Immortals speak.

It’s a suppression by realm!

The discourse has been hugely beneficial for both parties.

Song Shuhang has gained a wealth of knowledge about the Mysterious Principles of Immortality from many Immortal big shots. With these other mountains’ stones, he could perfect his own Second Immortality.

As expected of Tyrannical Song, what profound insights and extensive knowledge!

This was genuinely a ‘fortunate opportunity’!

Had they known this would be the result, they wouldn’t have needed Tyrannical Song’s fat ball manifestation to force them; they would have come willingly.

After this wave of debate and speech... Tyrannical Song’s prestige in the myriad practitioners in the universe will ascend another step!

Hidden in the shadows, Daozi’s senior brother revealed a satisfied smile.

He was secretly aiding Tyrannical Song’s next step in proving his pseudo-immortal body, gently pushing the waves.

Moreover, his method was like the spring rain, nourishing things quietly.

Not leave such a great pressure for the juniors.

Even if slacking off, he still has things he wants to do.

Chapter 3025: Chapter 3023: It’s Onion, I Added Onion!

Not understanding, not hearing clearly, didn’t affect the process.

Chapter 3037: Chapter 3035: Are You Changing Clothes?

Chapter 3038: Chapter 3036: Is It Still Resurrection If You Can’t Resurrect On the Spot?

Chapter 3039: Chapter 3037: Devouring Netherworld Ruler!

What’s even more wonderful is that with the “Confucian Classic” present, when Senior White is ready to inherit the Scholarly Sage’s Eye, he can complete the ritual by using up Song Shuhang’s “path to immortality” — just like how the Sage Secret Technique almost depleted Daoist Senior’s “immortal path” previously.

His own daughter, disciples, and members of the Nine Provinces Number One Group are all potential inheritors.

After the sacrificial ritual is completed, Song Shuhang himself can retain fragments of the “path to immortality”.

Text and language are the most fundamental aspects of the “Cultivator Chat System”.

And Song Shuhang’s true “Second Immortality” will use the “Cultivator Chat System” as its main framework.

Moreover, he has some leads on the next “path to immortality” he wants to sacrifice — he plans to create a highly inclusive way to immortality, connecting all the members of the Nine Provinces Number One Group.

Both of these options are the escalation of the “Cultivator Chat System” network cables and can connect him to the members of the Nine Provinces Number One Group.

Once the new way to immortality is established, he can sacrifice the “Language Text Longevity Technique” to Senior White, allowing Senior White to inherit the Sage’s Devouring Talent.

“Very good, everything is going smoothly just as I deduced using Daoist Senior’s predictive ability,” Song Shuhang said, reaching out to touch his blinded left eye socket.

The “undying revival” power of the fat whale golden core was activated.

The pendants on Tyrannical Song were not for show.

Chapter 3046: Chapter 3044: So, Physically Whitewash the Fat Ball

Just like Father Goudan at this moment, he could leave the Netherworld Realm at any time and go to the main world... However, once he left the Netherworld Realm, his existence would be severed from it, and he would be unable to return to the Netherworld in a short period.

Then, like Father Goudan, he would rely on the strength of others to penetrate the Netherworld with a strand of consciousness and return home to have a look.

Therefore, Dark Song was not in a hurry to move out of the ‘Netherworld Realm’—after all, whether it was the Heavenly Dao or the Netherworld Realm, both were on his side.

Heavenly Dao would not target him, and Senior White from the Netherworld certainly wouldn’t deal with him either.

He did not need to hide in the main world as Father Goudan did.

The fat ball was now extremely weak!

But it also turned misfortune into a blessing... As Dark Song was reborn by Fairy Cheng Lin, its connection with the Heavenly Dao was also severed.

Subsequently, even if Daoist Senior stepped down from the ‘Heavenly Dao seat’, this remaining part of the fat ball would not dissipate due to the collapse of the Heavenly Dao.

It’s just that because it had lost nine-tenths of its ‘existence’ to the ‘Sage’s talent,’ the fat ball was now in a long slumber and would probably struggle to recover for thousands or tens of thousands of years—it didn’t want to sleep; it had wanted to grit its teeth and hold on until it escaped danger and infiltrated a safe place to hide and recover.

But it was too weak... Not only was nine-tenths of its ‘existence’ taken away, but even its physical body was largely excised by Daozi, taken away to be purified, and prepared to create more ‘Song fat ball cloaks’ raw materials for Song Shuhang.

Thus, although the will of the fat ball was strong, its body was weak. Ultimately, it could not hold out and, just before the moment of victory, fell unwillingly into a long slumber.

“Senior Brother Daozi, what do you plan to do with the remaining part of the fat ball?” Dark Song asked aloud.

The manifested Heavenly Dao Will responded, “I promised it that as long as it cooperated voluntarily, I would not seal it again, nor would I restrict its freedom, letting it continue to live. Since it has done so... I will not break my promise.”

A gentleman’s agreement is heavier than a mountain.

Well...

A white ball doesn’t seem as attractive as a black ball?

Moreover, white is fattening.

Seeing how corpulent the fat ball already seemed, would it give off the impression of being too fat if it turned white?

Among them, there’s the authority to manually change ‘a portion of the ruler of the Netherworld’s memories.’ Looks like it will come in handy!”

This was a new Heavenly Dao’s function he had just stumbled upon, so he brought it out to show off.

Senior White Two’s projected clone, the Three-Eyed Sovereign, and Father Goudan involuntarily rubbed their temples with their hands or dragon mustaches.

As a companion, Fat Ball turns into the most considerate being... It is clever, thoughtful, caring, and incredibly capable—a single ball is more useful than ten clones.
